\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Note\+: some refactoring is needed. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_xsheet_viewer}{Xsheet\+Viewer}} is going to derive from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_spreadsheet_viewer}{Spreadsheet\+Viewer}}.

convert the last one digit of the frame number to alphabet Ex. 12 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 1B 21 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2A 30 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 3
